# <a name="sharepoint-online-service-description"></a><span data-ttu-id="649a9-104">SharePoint Online 服務說明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-104">SharePoint Online Service Description</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="649a9-105">Office 365 中的 Microsoft SharePoint Online 提供每個人共用和共同作業、通知和聯繫整個公司的其他人員、轉換商務流程，以及充分利用集體知識的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-105">Microsoft SharePoint Online in Office 365 empowers people to share and work together, to inform and engage others across the company, to transform business processes, and to harness collective knowledge.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-106">此外，SharePoint 還提供組織保護和管理資料，並建立自訂解決方案的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-106">In addition, SharePoint provides capabilities for organizations to protect and manage data and to build custom solutions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-107">如需快速概觀，請參閱[什麼是 SharePoint？](https://support.office.com/article/97b915e6-651b-43b2-827d-fb25777f446f)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-107">For a quick overview of other Microsoft SharePoint Online products and technologies, see [What is SharePoint?](https://support.office.com/article/97b915e6-651b-43b2-827d-fb25777f446f)</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="649a9-108">若要跨方案比較功能，請參閱[比較商務用 Office 365 方案 ](https://products.office.com/business/compare-more-office-365-for-business-plans)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-108">To compare features across plans, see [Compare Office 365 for Business plans](https://products.office.com/business/compare-more-office-365-for-business-plans).</span></span>
  
## <a name="whats-new"></a><span data-ttu-id="649a9-109">新功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-109">What's new</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="649a9-110">如需有關 SharePoint Online 新增功能的資訊，請參閱 [SharePoint Online 的新增功能](https://support.office.com/article/02449ef0-027e-4089-8717-f0ae7ea58029)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-110">For information about new features in SharePoint Online, see [What's new in SharePoint Online](https://support.office.com/article/02449ef0-027e-4089-8717-f0ae7ea58029).</span></span>
  
## <a name="system-requirements"></a><span data-ttu-id="649a9-111">系統需求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-111">System requirements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="649a9-112">如需適用於企業、教育和政府組織的 Office 365 每月訂閱型服務的系統需求，請參閱 [Office 365 系統需求](https://products.office.com/office-system-requirements/#Office365forBEG)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-112">For system requirements for Office 365, the monthly subscription-based service available for business, education, and government organizations, please see [Office 365 system requirements](https://products.office.com/office-system-requirements/#Office365forBEG).</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-p103">組織可以部署一個由 SharePoint Server 2013 或 2016 (一般是在內部部署) 和 SharePoint Online 組成的混合式 SharePoint 環境。若要深入了解，請參閱 [SharePoint Server 2013 的混合](https://docs.microsoft.com/SharePoint/hybrid/hybrid) 或 [SharePoint Server 2016 的混合](https://docs.microsoft.com/SharePoint/hybrid/hybrid)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-p103">An organization can deploy a hybrid SharePoint environment, which is composed of SharePoint Server 2013 or 2016, typically deployed on-premises, and SharePoint Online. To learn more, see [Hybrid for SharePoint Server 2013](https://docs.microsoft.com/SharePoint/hybrid/hybrid) or [Hybrid for SharePoint Server 2016](https://docs.microsoft.com/SharePoint/hybrid/hybrid).</span></span> 
  
## <a name="sharepoint-online-boundaries-and-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="649a9-115">SharePoint Online 界限和限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-115">SharePoint Online boundaries and limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="649a9-116">由 Microsoft 管理的 SharePoint Online服務有幾項限制，例如網站集合配額、檔案上傳限制和儲存限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-116">There are some limitations to the SharePoint Online service, such as site collection quotas, file upload limits, and storage limits.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-117">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 [SharePoint Online 限制](sharepoint-online-limits.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-117">For details, see [SharePoint Online Limits](sharepoint-online-limits.md).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="649a9-118">若要深入了解行動支援，請參閱[使用行動裝置在 SharePoint Online 網站上工作](https://support.office.com/article/a99f2acf-381a-442c-b305-3e74c251bcb6)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-118">To learn more about mobile support, see [Use a mobile device to work with SharePoint Online sites](https://support.office.com/article/a99f2acf-381a-442c-b305-3e74c251bcb6).</span></span>
  
## <a name="subscription-options"></a><span data-ttu-id="649a9-119">訂閱選項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-119">Subscription options</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="649a9-p105">我們在多種計劃中提供 Office 365 以盡可能滿足組織的需求。如需各種計劃的相關資訊 (包括獨立計劃選項和從某個計劃移動到其他計劃的資訊)，請參閱 Office 365 計劃選項[Office 365 方案選項](../office-365-platform-service-description/office-365-plan-options.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-p105">Office 365 is available in a variety of plans to best meet the needs of your organization. For information about different plans, including standalone plan options and information on moving from one plan to another, see [Office 365 Plan Options](../office-365-platform-service-description/office-365-plan-options.md).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="649a9-122">必須為每一位存取 SharePoint Online 的使用者指派 Office 365 方案，或是 SharePoint Online方案 1 或 SharePoint Online 方案 2 獨立服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-122">Each person who accesses SharePoint Online must be assigned to an Office 365 plan or SharePoint Online Plan 1 or SharePoint Online Plan 2 standalone service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-123">不過，第一線方案並不單獨出售，只能作為第一線訂閱的一部分，例如 SharePoint Online 第一線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-123">However, a kiosk plan is not sold as a standalone offer, only as part of the Kiosk subscription, such as SharePoint Online Kiosk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-124">因為第一線員工不能是系統管理員，所以具有第一線員工的租用戶至少需要有一個 Enterprise 系統管理員來管理 SharePoint。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-124">Since kiosk users can't be administrators, tenants with kiosk users require at least one Enterprise administrator to manage SharePoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-125">第一線員工看不到 SharePoint 導覽功能表，所以第一線員工必須直接藉由 URL 瀏覽至 SharePoint 網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-125">Kiosk users won't see SharePoint navigation menus, so kiosk users have to navigate to SharePoint sites directly by URL.</span></span>
  
## <a name="onedrive-for-business"></a><span data-ttu-id="649a9-126">商務用 OneDrive</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-126">OneDrive for Business</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="649a9-127">商務用 OneDrive (先前稱為 SkyDrive Pro) 適用於公司員工的個人線上儲存空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-127">OneDrive for Business (formerly SkyDrive Pro) is personal online storage for a company's employees.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-128">在這裡，使用者可以輕鬆並安全地跨多個裝置來儲存、同步及分享工作檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-128">It's the place where people can store, sync, and share their work files across multiple devices with ease and security.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-129">商務用 OneDrive 隨附於 SharePoint Online，但也可以作為獨立計劃另外購買。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-129">OneDrive for Business is included in SharePoint Online and can also be purchased as a standalone plan.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-130">商務用 OneDrive 獨立選項包括網頁版 Office。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-130">The OneDrive for Business standalone option includes Office Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-131">若要查看搭配網頁版 Office 之商務用 OneDrive 所包含的功能，請參閱 [商務用 OneDrive 服務說明](../onedrive-for-business-service-description.md) (部分內容機器翻譯)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-131">To see which features are included in OneDrive for Business with Office Online, see the [OneDrive for Business Service Description](../onedrive-for-business-service-description.md).</span></span>
  
## <a name="sharepoint-online-enterprise-external-users"></a><span data-ttu-id="649a9-132">SharePoint Online Enterprise 外部使用者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-132">SharePoint Online Enterprise external users</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="649a9-p108">外部使用者繼承邀請他們共同作業之 SharePoint Online 客戶的使用權限。亦即，如果組織購買 E3 Enterprise 計劃，並建置使用企業功能的網站，則會將使用和 (或) 檢視邀請它們加入之網站集合內企業功能的權限授與外部使用者。雖然外部使用者可以受邀為延伸專案成員以執行網站的完整範圍動作，但是他們的功能與組織內的完整已付費授權成員不完全相同。深入了解[為您的 SharePoint Online 環境管理外部共用](https://docs.microsoft.com/sharepoint/external-sharing-overview)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-p108">External users inherit the use rights of the SharePoint Online customer who is inviting them to collaborate. That is, if an organization purchases an E3 Enterprise plan and builds a site that uses enterprise features, the external user is granted rights to use and/or view the enterprise features within the site collection they are invited to. While external users can be invited as extended project members to perform a full range of actions on a site, they will not have the exact same capabilities as a full, paid, licensed member within your organization. Learn more about [what external users can and can't do](https://docs.microsoft.com/sharepoint/external-sharing-overview).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="649a9-1802"><sup>1</sup> 若要使用資料夾同步處理，您必須擁有 Office 2013 或更新版本 (標準版或專業版)，或是包含 Office 應用程式的 Office 365 訂閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1802"><sup>1</sup> To use folder sync, you must have Office 2013 or later (Standard or Professional edition) or an Office 365 subscription that includes Office applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-1803">Office 365 商務基本版、Office 365 Enterprise E1 以及 Office 365 教育版 方案並未包含 Office 桌面應用程式訂閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1803">Office 365 Business Essentials, Office 365 Enterprise E1, and Office 365 Education plans do not include subscriptions to Office desktop applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-1804">不過，如果您已安裝 Office 2013 或更新版本，並訂閱上述其中一個方案，就可以使用資料夾同步處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1804">However, you can use folder sync if you have Office 2013 or later installed and subscribe to one of these plans.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="649a9-1805"><sup>2</sup> 第一線員工可使用的商務用 OneDrive 功能有限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1805"><sup>2</sup> Kiosk users have limited OneDrive for Business functionality.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-1806">第一線員工得到 2GB 儲存體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1806">Firstline workers receive 2GB of storage.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="649a9-1807"> 
<sup>3</sup>Azure 資訊保護未包含在內，但是能以個別的附加元件形式購買，並且會啟用支援的資訊版權管理 (IRM) 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1807"> 
<sup>3</sup>Azure Information Protection is not included, but can be purchased as a separate add-on and will enable the supported Information Rights Management (IRM) features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-1808">Some Azure Information Protection features require a subscription to Office 365 ProPlus, which is not included with Office 365 Business Essentials, Office 365 Business Premium, Office 365 Enterprise E1, Office 365 Education, or Office 365 Enterprise F1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1808">Some Azure Information Protection features require a subscription to Office 365 ProPlus, which is not included with Office 365 Business Essentials, Office 365 Business Premium, Office 365 Enterprise E1, Office 365 Education, or Office 365 Enterprise F1.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="649a9-1809"><sup>4</sup> 因為第一線員工不能是系統管理員，所以具有第一線員工的租用戶至少必須有一個 Enterprise 使用者，才能存取系統管理中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1809"><sup>4</sup> Because Kiosk users can't be administrators, tenants with Kiosk users need at least one Enterprise user to access the admin center.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="649a9-1810"><sup>5</sup> SharePoint Online 客戶必須下載並安裝免費的排名模型調整應用程式，才能建立及自訂排名模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1810"><sup>3</sup> SharePoint Online customers need to download and install the free Rank Model Tuning App in order to create and customize ranking models.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="649a9-1811"> 
<sup>6</sup> 當您使用 eDiscovery 功能時，允許此功能的計劃授權要求會套用至所有屬於 eDiscovery 動作 (搜尋、保留、匯出) 的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1811"> 
<sup>6</sup> When you use eDiscovery features, the licensing requirement for a plan that permits that feature applies to all end users that are part of the eDiscovery action (Search, Hold, Export).</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="649a9-1812"><sup>7</sup> 已驗證的 SharePoint Online 使用者可以使用多面向導覽存取私用網站集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1812"><sup>7</sup> Authenticated SharePoint Online users can access private site collections with faceted navigation.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="649a9-1813"><sup>8</sup> 在您的國家/地區中，某些提供者可能被封鎖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1813"><sup>8</sup> Some providers may be blocked in your country/region.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="649a9-1814"> 
<sup>9</sup> 使用電子郵件與組織外的任何人共用文件、程式庫或網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1814"> 
<sup>9</sup> Sharing a document, library, or site by email with someone outside of your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-1815">系統管理員還是能夠將它開啟，但會出現警告訊息，指出它可能在您的國家/地區外進行檔案共用存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1815">Administrators do have the ability to turn it on, but will get a warning message indicating that it could make files shared accessible outside of your country.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-1816">嘗試與組織外部的其他人共用的使用者會收到相同的警告訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1816">Users who attempt to share with someone outside of the organization will receive the same warning message.</span></span> <br/>

<span data-ttu-id="649a9-1832"><sup>18</sup> F1 的使用者可以在混合式設定中存取 SharePoint Server，但 Office 365 F1 不包含 CAL 權限來存取伺服器；這些權限必須另外購買。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1832">F1 users can access SharePoint Server in a hybrid setup, but Office 365 F1 does not include CAL rights to access the server; these rights must be purchased separately.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="649a9-1833"><sup>19</sup> Office 365 企業版 E5 中提供客戶金鑰。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1833"><sup>19</sup> Customer Key is available in Office 365 Enterprise E5.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-1834">客戶金鑰可讓您控制貴組織的加密金鑰，然後設定 Office 365 使用這些金鑰來加密存放在 Microsoft 資料中心中的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1834">Customer Key enables you to control your organization's encryption keys and then configure Office 365 to use them to encrypt your data at rest in Microsoft's data centers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-1835">存放的資料包括 Exchange Online 資料和儲存在信箱的商務用 Skype 資料，以及儲存在 SharePoint Online 中和商務用 OneDrive 中的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1835">Data at rest includes data from Exchange Online and Skype for Business that is stored in mailboxes and files that are stored in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-1836">客戶金鑰可協助您符合規範，因為您可以控制加密金鑰，Office 365 會使用該金鑰來解密資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1836">Customer Key helps you meet compliance obligations because you control the encryption keys that Office 365 uses to decrypt data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="649a9-1837">如需相關資訊，請參閱 [使用客戶金鑰控制 Office 365 中的資料](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/controlling-your-data-using-customer-key)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="649a9-1837">For more information, see [Controlling your data in Office 365 using Customer Key](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/securitycompliance/controlling-your-data-using-customer-key).</span></span> <br/>
